  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_e5c5de83-d6da-4cde-ab40-b3bb02f10616'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer813050025112951988">Lilli Accardo moves to the dying town of Signal Bend, Missouri, where the citizens have made a devil’s bargain to stay afloat. Lilli quickly garners the attention of the whole town, particularly Isaac Lunden, President of the Night Horde Motorcycle Club and de facto protector of the town and its citizens. <br/><br/>When it turns out that Lilli is there under murky circumstances, Isa</span>
  <span id="freeText813050025112951988" style="display:none">Lilli Accardo moves to the dying town of Signal Bend, Missouri, where the citizens have made a devil’s bargain to stay afloat. Lilli quickly garners the attention of the whole town, particularly Isaac Lunden, President of the Night Horde Motorcycle Club and de facto protector of the town and its citizens. <br /><br />When it turns out that Lilli is there under murky circumstances, Isaac decides to get close and try to figure out what she’s hiding. Their chemistry is instantaneous and electric, but each is a potential danger to the other. <br /><br />Action, sex, and drama ensue as Isaac and Lilli try to navigate the rocky terrain between trust and threat. <br /><br /><i><b>Note:</b> explicit sex and violence. </i></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/840046619?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer840046619" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16824193198800798293"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391337696i/8375003._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>Well-worn black engineer boots. Dark straight-leg Levis. Black button-down shirt, folded back on his arms and open at the throat. Leather cuffs. Leather kutte. Black Ray-Bans. He looked like Mr. June in the Harley biker Beefcake calendar</b>
</blockquote><br/>Yeah, yeah, I hear you say, “another biker book”! Yes, it was a biker book but so much more. I cannot believe I got this gem of a book FREE back in December. As with nearly ALL my free books, they stay on my kindle… usually never seeing the light of day again</span>
  <span id="freeText16824193198800798293" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391337696i/8375003._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>Well-worn black engineer boots. Dark straight-leg Levis. Black button-down shirt, folded back on his arms and open at the throat. Leather cuffs. Leather kutte. Black Ray-Bans. He looked like Mr. June in the Harley biker Beefcake calendar</b>
</blockquote><br>Yeah, yeah, I hear you say, “another biker book”! Yes, it was a biker book but so much more. I cannot believe I got this gem of a book FREE back in December. As with nearly ALL my free books, they stay on my kindle… usually never seeing the light of day again. Not this one!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391337696i/8375004._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>Women with big purses freaked him out. What the fuck was so important they had to carry a damn suitcase with them everywhere they went?</b>
</blockquote><br>This was the story of Isaac and Lilli. Lilli arrives in town, she catches the eye of Isaac, who is the President of the local Motorcycle Club. But this story was not out to shock me. I do think a lot of the MC books like to throw in the shock factor, the gritty scenes… Granted there were some gritty scenes here but not like some of the other books I read.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387728555ra/7659030.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Fuck, you have a great cock," she whispered.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>I don’t want to say much as I think you should just go and read it without knowing too much about it. There is an instant attraction between Isaac and Lilli. I think Lilli must be one of the strongest heroines I have read about. She knew what she wanted and she took no shit from anyone.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391337696i/8375005.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Jesus, you’re prickly. No. It means I know I like you more than just a fuck. I think there’s something happening here. I think you feel it too. I want to play that out a little."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>As I said I don’t want to say much. Yes, Lilli is hiding something, yes there are background stories that all intermingle. Great book, look forward to the next in the series.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391337696i/8375006._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>EVEN SWEET, THOUGH, HE STILL MADE HER SCREAM</b>
</blockquote><br></span>

From an economical point, Signal Bend is a very crisis-ridden town and Lilli moving here stirs up some interesting quest</span>
  <span id="freeText17659467649999876524" style="display:none"><b>4 f@ck-me-rough stars. Review completed March 31, 2014</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395929144ra/9063525.gif" alt=" photo oie_l1ITpNXYSHWF_zpsc767b66b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395929144ra/9063526.gif" alt=" photo oie_mzrQZgXu8Xja_zps3bf8dc0a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395929144ra/9063527.gif" alt=" photo oie_gvpMBYqVL4Y7_zpsc2bceb59.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When an attractive yet mysterious woman rents a place in Signal Bend, Isaac Lunden, President of the Night Horde Motorcycle Club, casts an eye at the sexy woman when she turns up at a town's dive. They share a meal together, have some 'fun' in the form of a little brawl and continue to have some more fun between the sheets. From an economical point, Signal Bend is a very crisis-ridden town and Lilli moving here stirs up some interesting questions. Isaac is more than willing to combine the sexy pleasure with the serious matter.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Are you asking me on a date? Won't the town gossips have a field day?"<br>"Baby, they started hearing wedding bells when they saw us at Marie's. I'm not known to feed my fucks. There's nothing we could do to stir them up more--unless I knock you up, which I have no intention of doin'.</b>

  <b>
    <i>"I think we're getting to know each other in the important ways first." He lifted her hand to his mouth for a kiss. His lips still brushing the back of her hand, he said. "You amaze me, Lilli. I'm not afraid to say I'm gettin' caught up here."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This goes both ways, though. Isaac amazes Lilli too. He's a bearded badass biker hunk, incredibly tall, ripped, broad-shouldered with very long and thick hair with a penchant for <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[artistry. As a matter of fact, Isaac is a very gifted craftsman <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and if I hadn't fallen for him already I would have when I knew that his hands are not only good to bring tough Lilli to screaming orgasms, but he also knows how to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[craft beautiful wooden furniture and decoration objects. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> To top everything off, Isaac is a very well-read man. Me likey. Very much so.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396022061ra/9077970.gif" alt=" photo oie_nhcnUfOq1roC_zps5730b074.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>

  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396022061ra/9077971.gif" alt=" photo oie_8OHpH7QQtiOx_zpsf84e25dd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Jesus fuck, you feel good," he breathed. She didn't say anything. She was too wrapped up in the amazing feel of this night, of him sliding inside her. Moaning, she tipped her head back, and he latched on, suckling at her throat, then kissing along her shoulder where the surface of the lake lapped at her.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Not so long ago I've had a chat with my friend Kels and she was talking about how much fun she's had by reading Susan Fanetti's Signal Bend series. After having experienced another train wreck together with my friend and buddy reader Glamdring, we were both in dire need of a good read. We decided to give this series a shot and I must say it was worth my time and money! Yowza. I'm back in a very good place and I'm positive that some good reads lay ahead of me in the foreseeable future.<br><br>I liked Lilli very much. She was right up my alley because she's the opposite of an idiotic and screeching biker babe. Lilli is used to give as good as she gets and then some. She's a very well-educated, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(she has a Bachelor of Arts in Renaissance History and a Bachelor of Arts in Middle Eastern Studies) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> polylingual <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(Lilli speaks eight languages) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and strong woman who has nothing much to lose anymore. She's quite experienced sexually but not so much in the matters of the heart and hasn't settled down yet. She sure as heck hadn't expected that to happen when she set foot in Signal Bend for the first time, though. But things never turn out the way you expect anyway. I must say that I was more than a little bit thrilled when I knew more about Lilli's background and realized what a badass chick this woman is. Lilli <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[flew Blackhawk helicopters for the US Army. However, after a specific "incident" in Afghanistan, she was honorably discharged and shortly afterward she started to train and work for the NSA. Now she's doing highly classified contract work and a very personal assignment led her to Signal Bend. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Move the Sun is a fast-paced and very engaging read that provides lots of sex (a bit too much for my tastes actually); it is funny in places and rather gritty and violent in others. A couple scenes made me wince, i.e. Isaac <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ramming scissors in the realtor's hand or removing someone's fingernails <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> is honestly not my kind of fun but I've got to deal with it. Bikers are no angels, after all. Friendly heads up, the f@cks are definitely on the <b>rougher</b> side, but as long as both parties love to play it wild all is fine. Anyway, they are real good at what they're doing and might achieve to rev up your libido as well. Mission accomplished, right? In consequence, smut lovers will get their money's worth, but also those readers who enjoy a good story will most likely end up pleased.<br><br><b>Bottom line</b><br>Move the Sun combines the hot as fuck sex with a hot as fuck hunk of a hero and a sexy and <b>tough</b> as fuck heroine and a really well-developed storyline. Satisfaction guaranteed. Pun intended.<br><br>Go read it!<br><br><br>Recommended read.<br><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://baba.booklikes.com">http://baba.booklikes.com</a><br><br><br>****************<br><br>Buddy read with my lovely friend Glamdring! I enjoyed it--thank you!! &lt;333 xxx </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="17659467649999876524" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</i><br/>I have so many trusted friends who love Susan Fanetti and this series, so I knew I needed to read it. When I saw the author was attending a signing near me this summer, I knew I needed to bump it up on my TBR. I'm so happy I did. It's been a while since I've read a biker book this good. It hooked me from the start, and now that I'm invested, I want to read allllll the books in this series! <br/><br/>When Lilli enters the small town of Signal </span>
  <span id="freeText7115702627768892622" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1523448364i/25359239._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="“description”/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “The love which moves the sun and the other stars.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>I have so many trusted friends who love Susan Fanetti and this series, so I knew I needed to read it. When I saw the author was attending a signing near me this summer, I knew I needed to bump it up on my TBR. I'm so happy I did. It's been a while since I've read a biker book this good. It hooked me from the start, and now that I'm invested, I want to read allllll the books in this series! <br><br>When Lilli enters the small town of Signal Bend, she's on a mission. The last thing she's looking for is a man. But then she sees Isaac. Isaac is the President of the local MC and I think it's fair to say they both catch each others eye right away. There is a pull between them and their chemistry is undeniable. Even though neither one of them are 'relationship' people, they can't stay away. <br><br><i>Move the Sun</i> is different from the normal MC book in a lot of ways. It's deeper. As much as I loved our biker Isaac, Lilli completely stole the show for me. Talk about a bad ass heroine! She shocked me more than once and I just loved her! <br><br>This is one of those books that I'm kicking myself for waiting so long to read. It's gritty, suspenseful, action packed, and super hot. It's also very well written. I can't wait to read more from this author and I'm jumping in to book 2 straight away. </span>

She moved to Single Bend and everyone is curious about her because no one moves to this small rundown town. She is immediately on Isaac's radar. <br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/39800747-33C7-4F10-8892-8DB0964A5E03_zps759d0kxt.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469197114ra/19791648.gif" alt=" photo 39800747-33C7-4F10-8892-8DB0964A5E03_zps759d0kxt.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Isaac is the Night Horde MC president and pretty much runs the town. He makes everything in Single Bend his clubs business. He is one sexy badass mother fucker. He is curious as to why Lilli is there and immediately starts trying to get in her business.<br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/85F8A999-7F7F-419D-942A-23EA917916EC_zpssyxf7vru.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469197114ra/19791649.gif" alt=" photo 85F8A999-7F7F-419D-942A-23EA917916EC_zpssyxf7vru.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>The attraction between these two is friggin hot and the sex is smoking. They fight and they take that fighting into the bedroom. They go hard and fast and it's perfect!<br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/5E657496-D72A-4055-AE32-486CA5872785_zpsnfir36h3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469197114ra/19791650.gif" alt=" photo 5E657496-D72A-4055-AE32-486CA5872785_zpsnfir36h3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>As they start trusting one another, we find out why Lilli is there and it is most definitely not because she loves the little country town. <br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/37BB713A-F5D1-4346-824A-89DCA463399F_zps90siigkm.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469197114ra/19791651.gif" alt=" photo 37BB713A-F5D1-4346-824A-89DCA463399F_zps90siigkm.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>So excited that April recommended this series. Moving on to book three. I can't wait for more Lilli and Issac!!<br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/3100872C-BF19-4059-9A23-53AD212A1E53_zpstneeei1q.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>Okay.. One more because Sons of Anarchy was the best show ever!!!<br><br><a href="http://s304.photobucket.com/user/dwoods5/media/4900C4DC-BA68-436E-919A-37B2B3FBCBB8_zpsxmlem0e2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <span id="freeText13991561461592692016" style="display:none">4.5--<b>Why Did I Wait So Long To Read This</b>--Stars!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386088458ra/7289006.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is definitely one of my most favorite MC books/series...and I can't wait to read more about Issac and Lilli and the other Horde members. <br><br>First and foremost...Lilli was a <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428780ra/858246.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383151768ra/6417483.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One of my most favorite heroines ever.<br><br>And Isaac was <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396979280ra/9213379.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He was the perfect mix of sweet and asshole. He wasn't afraid to go after what he wanted and he was honest about how he felt about Lilli from the get-go. <br><br>The sex in this book....OH. MY. JEEBUS. It was HOT!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396980464ra/9213535.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lilli is new to Signal Bend...she's blown in with her fancy car, and unassuming looks...and Isaac immediately takes notice. <br><br>Signal Bend is his town. And no one moves in to Signal Bend.<br><br>There's an immdediate attraction between Isaac and Lilli. But I loved both Isaac and Lilli. I loved how their relationship grew and they learned to trust each other. There was no unnecessary, immature drama. Just two people whose paths crossed, that fell in love when they weren't looking for it or expecting it. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I love you, Sport. You’re it for me. You fill up a space in me I didn’t even know was empty.”</blockquote>
</b> <br>This was more of a HFN type ending, I suppose. There was no cliffie. <br><br>But there are some parts of the plot that are left unresolved (Issac and Lilli's story continues in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19266169.Behold_the_Stars__Signal_Bend___2_" title="Behold the Stars (Signal Bend, #2) by Susan Fanetti" rel="nofollow noopener">Behold the Stars</a>). Move the Sun was more about Lilli and her past, while the next book focuses more on Isaac and the Night Horde Motorcycle Club.<br><br>Definitely recommend for any MCs lovers out there! </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer851767133" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1827965090416194222"><br/>★★★★ <b>4 Stars!</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397586365i/9296855.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i><b>"L'amor che muove il sole e l'altre stelle."</b><br/>"The love which moves the sun and the other stars."</i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397586365ra/9296856.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Move the Sun</b> was a fun, fast-paced, action-filled, hot, original story that I very much enjoyed reading. I love a good biker book, especially when they're done right, and this one was right up my alley. But <i>Move the Sun</i> was so much more than "just" another biker book. It has a solid varied plot that constantly kept me on the edge of my seat, a amazingly strong, feisty no-nonsense hero</span>
  <span id="freeText1827965090416194222" style="display:none"><br>★★★★ <b>4 Stars!</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397586365i/9296855.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i><b>"L'amor che muove il sole e l'altre stelle."</b><br>"The love which moves the sun and the other stars."</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397586365ra/9296856.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Move the Sun</b> was a fun, fast-paced, action-filled, hot, original story that I very much enjoyed reading. I love a good biker book, especially when they're done right, and this one was right up my alley. But <i>Move the Sun</i> was so much more than "just" another biker book. It has a solid varied plot that constantly kept me on the edge of my seat, a amazingly strong, feisty no-nonsense heroine and let's not forget - a bossy, controlling, sexy biker alpha male. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397823667i/9332767.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When <b>Lilli Accardo</b> moves to the small town of Signal Bend, Missouri she immediately gathers the attention of the entire town. Why would a 33 year old city girl move to a dying town in the middle of nowhere? What nobody knows, but what many people suspect, is that she's there on a mission. One that might possibly endanger the rest of the town which is why the town's protective guard and their charismatic leader Isaac Lunden has decided to keep a close eye on her...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397823667i/9332768._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Isaac Lunden</b> is the president of the Night Horde MC and unofficial authority figure in and around Signal Bend. He's the kind of guy who doesn't get attached and who enjoys his freedom and independency when it comes to women and relationships. In the bedroom, he's as raw and dirty as they come and Lilli has no problem keeping up with him. Beneath his rough exterior though - he has a soft and caring heart and the combination of those two aspects constantly made me either swoon or fan myself. <br><br>While Isaac and Lilli are slowly but surely getting to know each other better, the town of Signal Bend is under the attack of a vicious crime lord and the constant pressure to sell their properties and their lifelong homes so that crime can become it's sole resident there. The people of Signal Bend all depend on the power and protection of the Night Horde and it's up to Isaac to fight to protect their beloved home town.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Who do they want you to be?"<br><b>"A fucking savior."</b><br>"I don't know, love. I think maybe you saved me."</i>
</blockquote><br>I will not say much more about the rest of the storyline. Just know that there is never a dull moment throughout the entire story and that there's a perfect combination of action/suspense and romance. Also, there's <b>no cliffhanger</b>.<br><br>If you're in the mood for a "real", raw, gritty, sexy MC book, look no further - this book has it all! The MC's are wonderful together, they have the best chemistry and a strong solid connection (which is needed with all the chaos going on around them). I can't wait to read more about them and the rest of the Night Horde members in the rest of this series! :D<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397823667i/9332769.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You astound me."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1212602562" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3080524158604789397"><br/><b>
  <i>”Welcome to Signal Bend!”</i>
</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span> <br/><br/>Lilli Accardo moves to Signal Bend, Missouri for ‘work’ purposes. She has all sorts of plans but what she didn’t plan for is falling for the town’s motorcycle club president. Things get tricky when Lilli’s mission and Isaac’s attraction and curiosities collide. These two are powerhouses in their own right but together made one kick ass couple.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>”A man pays what he owes.”</i>
</b><br/> <br/>Isaac and Lilli were off the charts hot together (loved the yoga mat/tree scene).</span>
  <span id="freeText3080524158604789397" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>”Welcome to Signal Bend!”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span> <br><br>Lilli Accardo moves to Signal Bend, Missouri for ‘work’ purposes. She has all sorts of plans but what she didn’t plan for is falling for the town’s motorcycle club president. Things get tricky when Lilli’s mission and Isaac’s attraction and curiosities collide. These two are powerhouses in their own right but together made one kick ass couple.<br><br><b>
  <i>”A man pays what he owes.”</i>
</b><br> <br>Isaac and Lilli were off the charts hot together (loved the yoga mat/tree scene). Lilli is a great tough heroine, while Isaac won me over from the first page. I really loved the way he carried himself and put his feelings out there from the beginning. I also love his hobby and those show scenes. <br><br><b>
  <i>”That wasn’t sex talk, Lilli. I’m tellin’ you I love you. Don’t make a fuss. Just sayin’ what I feel.”</i>
</b><br><br>As for the big picture of what is coming to town it will definitely have readers one clicking book two of the series to see what happens next. Overall this is a good biker book that gifted readers a strong, loyal and wonderful President to back and a small town to protect. <br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_842547727" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/842547727" />
    <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts"><img alt="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591195447p2/16496589.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/842547727?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts?shelf=hot">hot</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer842547727" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7121805719508631921"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418832428i/12916857.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>What a ride.<br/>What a writer.<br/>This story is wonderful!<br/><br/><b>Move the Sun</b> is a story about honesty, loyalty, trust and the truth. It's an MC tale so, as one would expect, its raw in places and that rawness got me right in the feels. It has one of the best prologues I’ve ever had the pleasure of reading... The author totally sucked me in and cleverly made my emotions flow for Lili, the heroine. I felt sympathy, angst and heartache. How does one get through life after experiencing that kind of trauma?<br/><br/>Lili mo</span>
  <span id="freeText7121805719508631921" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418832428i/12916857.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What a ride.<br>What a writer.<br>This story is wonderful!<br><br><b>Move the Sun</b> is a story about honesty, loyalty, trust and the truth. It's an MC tale so, as one would expect, its raw in places and that rawness got me right in the feels. It has one of the best prologues I’ve ever had the pleasure of reading... The author totally sucked me in and cleverly made my emotions flow for Lili, the heroine. I felt sympathy, angst and heartache. How does one get through life after experiencing that kind of trauma?<br><br>Lili moves to the small town of Signal Bend, home to Isaac's MC Brothers. There's an element of mystery, as to who she is and why she's there, which makes Lili even more alluring and, of course, there's a whole load of chemistry going on.... <i>raw sexual want and desire.</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418849840i/12921933._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Isaac is the MC President and most influential man in town. He takes his duty as town protector extremely seriously... He's powerful, intelligent and as tough, hard and brutal as MC's come... He’s, <b>“…the complete package.”</b> <br><br>In terms of appearance Isaac wouldn't be my go-to kind of guy with his long hair and beard but boy does Susan Fanetti make him completely appealing in every way. She writes Isaac’s physicality in a stunning manner giving him immense book presence. His introduction gave me the book tingles, I fell in lust with him... <b>“She couldn’t recall the last time she’d been so viscerally attracted to another human being.” </b>....<i>and then I fell in love.</i> I felt their intense attraction to each other….. The way Lili describes him, through her eyes and in her thoughts is so enticing and creates the most charismatic picture. The sexy tantalizing descriptions of how they touch each other, hold and explore each other are delectable.<br><br><i>There first kiss is gorgeous.</i><br><br>There's an undeniable attraction that smolders on the page. I love their banter, their, "...verbal sparring," and the sex is wow! Hard. Erotic... sometimes rough, <b>always passionate</b> and so very, very lovely. They're both insatiable. I felt the equality in their fucking. She is thoroughly his match in EVERY way and, more importantly, he is hers<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418856497i/12923847._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There's no frills or drama for the sake of it It's naturalistic... There's character driven motivation in every detail, making them honest and tangible in their thoughts, words and actions. I love the way Isaac's musings are slightly broken at times. It gives an authentic vibe. It's as intense as it's subtle and the story constantly evolves in terms of the characters, plot and emotion.... Susan Fanetti's writing is perfect for me; she keeps it totally real and authentic. I could feel the emotion, see the happenings and hear the characters; it was like watching a movie. Her writing bombards the senses. <br><br>The small town mentality is completely evident. We get to meet the other MC Brothers who I know feature in their own story... I'm looking forward to becoming further acquainted with each and every one of them. <br><br>The way the story is structured, the telling of it with interludes is just perfection. They give the story provenance, show layers, depth and history, ultimately providing credible reason for everything the character's do. They take the reader to times in Lili’s life that directly affect her existence and current plans…. The interludes are enlightening and gripping and move the story forward in a totally captivating way. And the <b>Oh-My-Goodness</b> of the story comes at EXACTLY the right moment. <br><br><b>Move the Sun has the perfect dose of intrigue added to a mix of emotion and erotic love…. </b>It made my mind work over time...<i> How did it all connect? </i><br><br><b>There's a moment between the hero and heroine that moved me to tears, the words, the emotion, the feelings that this author emotes with her characters and words is spectacular.</b> I watched as Lili and Isaac devoured each other and evolved as people. The one unsolved mystery for me is why the average rating for this story is not higher? I cannot for the life of me fathom it. For me it's an outstanding read and moves this author into the automatic buy category. I highly recommend to all those seeking an MC book with truth in the telling and soul in the characters. <br><br><br>BR with Deanna PinkLady<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7121805719508631921" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer842475236" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer9870103791654227425"><b>5 -<i>By the Love that moves the sun and the other stars</i> - Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/MovetheSun_zps9df27f12.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Boy did this book blow me away. I have had several people tell me that I must this series. Well, my dear friend Jxxx won this book in a contest and she bequeathed it to me as she is in the UK. So together we started out our BR and we discovered together the amazing and phenomenal writing of Susan Fanetti.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/8b90181c8f2ed6b0c33bb5eb8228be73_zps9f927630.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>I am not much on motorcycle club books but this one is fantastic. The heroine and hero are incredible. Isaac, President of Ni</span>
  <span id="freeText9870103791654227425" style="display:none"><b>5 -<i>By the Love that moves the sun and the other stars</i> - Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/MovetheSun_zps9df27f12.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Boy did this book blow me away. I have had several people tell me that I must this series. Well, my dear friend Jxxx won this book in a contest and she bequeathed it to me as she is in the UK. So together we started out our BR and we discovered together the amazing and phenomenal writing of Susan Fanetti.<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/8b90181c8f2ed6b0c33bb5eb8228be73_zps9f927630.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I am not much on motorcycle club books but this one is fantastic. The heroine and hero are incredible. Isaac, President of Night Horde MC and Lilli, a woman with secrets, are a breathtaking couple; strong, feisty, sexy.....they can hold their own with each other. I love that they are both powerful in their own right. Lilli is one of the most fascinating heroines I have read about. Her strength and her commitment to her secret are inspiring and she can protect herself like nobody's business. Isaac is a powerful leader and protector. He cares and loves his Club and will not let anyone try to take them down. His strength, his swagger, his commitment makes him one sexy man. Their intense chemistry is way beyond the charts- the sex these two have is earth shaking.....(I couldn't put a gif that really showed their explosion for fear I would get flagged)<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/ec134aad446374e42d43d476043f6c81_zps964fd82d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417417924i/12349564.jpg" alt=" photo ec134aad446374e42d43d476043f6c81_zps964fd82d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It's hard to really review this book as there are secrets and discoveries and you should read in order to find them out. Telling you would spoil but I will say that from the beginning, Ms Fanetti sucks you in. This story has intrigue, suspense, great verbal bantering, and hot sex. The way the story unfolds will keep you completely immersed. Lilli shows up in Signal Bend, Missouri, renting a house. There is nothing going on in this dried up town but it's protected by the Night Horde Motorcycle Club. Isaac is the President of the club and he knows all that goes on in his town. From the moment he saw Lilli, there was something, they just clicked. The way their relationship develops is so real and honest. There is no unnecessary drama-the story is rich and deep and full of emotion. I loved getting to see them come together as a couple despite Lilli's secret. I loved how they both learned to trust one another and take a chance. I definitely can't wait to continue their story with the next book in the series.<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Quotes/c46a9c35c6b3b64b35922ada2d83a69b_zps41f1914d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417417924i/12349563._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo c46a9c35c6b3b64b35922ada2d83a69b_zps41f1914d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I must thank Irene and TeriLyn for adding another author to my favorite list. ♥♥♥<br><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer841157648" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1797311943463154102"><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&current=024b3798dbdbae15920e6c0a18578ce4_zps87b10da2.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391737418i/8446439._SY540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Four holy hotness biker stars! Move on over fellow biker books, there's a new biker series in town. Move the Sun has all the great elements of an MC-based book...hot biker guys, tough as nails club politics, a strong heroine, and hot hot steamy sex scenes. <br/><br/>Move the Sun doesn't waste much time heating up the pages. Isaac, president of Night Horde MC Club, spots the new chic in town immediately. It's his job to know everything that goes on in his town so it takes little time to get the info. o</span>
  <span id="freeText1797311943463154102" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=024b3798dbdbae15920e6c0a18578ce4_zps87b10da2.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391737418i/8446439._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Four holy hotness biker stars! Move on over fellow biker books, there's a new biker series in town. Move the Sun has all the great elements of an MC-based book...hot biker guys, tough as nails club politics, a strong heroine, and hot hot steamy sex scenes. <br><br>Move the Sun doesn't waste much time heating up the pages. Isaac, president of Night Horde MC Club, spots the new chic in town immediately. It's his job to know everything that goes on in his town so it takes little time to get the info. on her...which isn't much. She's got some serious information walls protecting her past. Even his IT guy can't get past it. Isaac will just have to go to the source. <br><br>Lilli has had a pretty tragic past, enduring the loss of both parents and her nonna...finding two of the three. She's coming to Signal Bend, a no-man town, on a top security project for her "job." She doesn't need anyone nosing around but this Isaac is hard to resist...and will definitely make being "low on the radar" difficult. Seems he runs the town more than the police. <br><br>This wasn't a case of complete insta-love but they clicked from the start physically. It sucked you in early on...with feelings following suit. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=c8cec1cf5cdd7267477314d37980c46d_zps99ee0511.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391737418i/8446440._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I really enjoyed this read. Writing was good, editing virtually flawless. It kept my interest and the heat in it was...ah. Really nice. My only beef with the story was a huge event towards the end being rather "breezed" over. It was pretty much the climax of the story and parts just weren't addressed in its resolution. It's vague but a total spoiler if I explain more. Don't click if you've not read the book. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Where were the cops after her altercation with Hopson? That was huge, and the body obviously was "taken care of." The law enforcement side of all that never was brought up beyond the doctor saying she called them so that really felt like a huge gap in the story for me, It was as if she had a word count limit and couldn't clear it up before the end. Hmm <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This is a series and it appears the next book is the same characters. Looking forward to more from this author. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=c88fdafe3da27c554d9ed0c6ccb13052_zps92bd4053.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391737418i/8446441.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer929074598" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5586965990325082503"><b> 4.5 Stars<br/><br/>"You amaze me Lilli. I'm not afraid to say I'm gettin' caught up here."</b><br/><br/>I. Loved. This. Book.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399471089i/9555731._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was my kind of MC book. It didn't try so damn hard to be badass. This is the mature, older brother badass biker book to the petulant little brother biker book with little man syndrome. These guys have a certain code of honor and respect for people other than themselves. Sure, there's a certain level of skank going on but that's life. It happens everywhere. <br/><br/>These guys have actual lives and l</span>
  <span id="freeText5586965990325082503" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 Stars<br><br>"You amaze me Lilli. I'm not afraid to say I'm gettin' caught up here."</b><br><br>I. Loved. This. Book.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399471089i/9555731._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was my kind of MC book. It didn't try so damn hard to be badass. This is the mature, older brother badass biker book to the petulant little brother biker book with little man syndrome. These guys have a certain code of honor and respect for people other than themselves. Sure, there's a certain level of skank going on but that's life. It happens everywhere. <br><br>These guys have actual lives and like to live them. It reminded me of Sons of Anarchy more than other MC books I've read. That's a good thing for me. The club helps with drug running, but keep it out of their town. Many of the guys are family men. Many of them grew up in this small Missouri farming town and are content to stay there. <br><br>Lilli...with less makeup/tattoos. She is a complete and total badass and if I liked girls, I'd be all over that.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399471089i/9555733._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Lilli is alone in the world. She's been wronged in many ways but her purpose in life right now is to right one of those wrongs. Vigilante mission? Oh, yeah. Can she handle it? Bet your ass!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399470450i/9555620._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To put it mildly, Lilli effing <u>rocks</u>. She's confident and beautiful but doesn't really care. She's not prissy and pissy. She's ex army and feels comfortable in her own skin. She's absolutely PERFECT for Isaac. <br><br><b>"You don't do the lime and salt thing, huh?"<br>"Not unless I'm looking for attention at a bar..."</b> and those of us who have read this know just how hilarious that sassy comment is because <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ this crazy bitch totally wins over the entire MC by strutting her sexy self into a bar, buying them all shots of tequila, and licking and sucking that salt and lime like a porn star!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Freaking cracked me up!<br><br>Isaac...MC prez, badass enough to handle Lilli, a nice guy underneath it all...<br><b>"He looked like Mr. June in the Harley Biker Beefcake calendar..."</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399471089i/9555732._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The best part of this book is how these two complement each other. The flat out fit, in every way imaginable...in the bedroom in particular, but also having random conversations, you see just how well they mesh. This town is really small, and everyone knows everyone. Lilli's arrival doesn't go unnoticed.<br><b>"Are you asking me on a date? Won't the town gossips have a field day?"<br>"Baby, they started hearing wedding bells when they saw us at Marie's. I'm not known to feed my fucks."</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399470450i/9555621.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦<br><br>Some favorite quotes:<br>♦♦ <b>"Damn, Sport. I don't want to sound all flowery, but I don't think I've ever had a fuck like that before. You're somethin' else."<br><br>♦♦ "At least try it. I promise you won't turn into a vegetarian if one meal doesn't have an animal in it."<br>He pulled his plate back. "Yeah, something tells me this is a gateway sandwich."<br><br>♦♦ "You're it for me. You fill up a space in me I didn't even know was empty."</b><br><br>♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦♦<br><br>Anyone who is hesitant about MC books...I AM TOO! But this is good stuff. There is ROMANCE EVERYWHERE, people. Even badasses love <b>someone</b>, even in real life! So yay on the romance and don't even get me started on the sex. Blow your head off sex, ROUGH and DIRTY and so hot. Lilli is a wildcat and not afraid to show that side of herself. We should all take lessons, for real. There's some suspense, some blood and action, a really fantastic plot but also a series arc that leaves you wondering about the next story. I highly recommend this book!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-contemporary">romance-m-f-contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1022477931" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15864957816471208024"><i>Written May 31, 2015</i><br/><br/><b>4.7 Stars - Stunning captivating, touching and romantic — this one "got" me</b><br/><br/><i>
  <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/116551-signal-bend' rel='nofollow noopener'>'Signal Bend'</a>
</i> is a m/f MC (bikers) series I've curiously peeked at for a while. Felt good to at last start this first installment to see if these could be MC-books in my (delicate picky) taste. <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Often I've a hard time to find contemporary m/f romances I sincerely like. I don't want YA, not just FSoG erotica or too sugary homey sweet stuff neither.  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> ~ Karen, Mo and man</span>
  <span id="freeText15864957816471208024" style="display:none"><i>Written May 31, 2015</i><br><br><b>4.7 Stars - Stunning captivating, touching and romantic — this one "got" me</b><br><br><i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/116551-signal-bend" rel="nofollow noopener">'Signal Bend'</a>
</i> is a m/f MC (bikers) series I've curiously peeked at for a while. Felt good to at last start this first installment to see if these could be MC-books in my (delicate picky) taste. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Often I've a hard time to find contemporary m/f romances I sincerely like. I don't want YA, not just FSoG erotica or too sugary homey sweet stuff neither.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> ~ Karen, Mo and many friends with them, loved this one (and some of the other parts) so why not try it.<br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/image.jpg3_zpseu1qf8sh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432608077i/14987802.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg3_zpseu1qf8sh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><b><i>“L’amor che muove il sole e l’altre stelle.”</i></b><br>(The love which moves the sun and the other stars.)<br><i>Dante ~ «The Divine Comedy»</i>
</blockquote><br><b>Wow, Hurrah, Yay!!</b><br><i>Move the Sun</i> was just PERFECT for this crancy Swedish Lady. I drank in every word, and just want more from Lilli &amp; Isaac's interesting —but scary— world. Looking forward to pick up book #2 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1294453566" rel="nofollow noopener">Behold the Stars</a>, the continuing sequel. <br><br>********************************************************* <br><br><i>Signal Bend, Missouri, U.S...</i><br>Stories set in a small Midwestern town called <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/116551-signal-bend" rel="nofollow noopener">Signal Bend</a> about the members in the <i>'Night Horde Motorcycle Club'</i>. This series (7 books) opener <i>Move The Sun</i> is the introduction to the towns newcomer <b>Lillian 'Lilli' Accardo</b>'s and the club president <b>Isaac 'Ike' Lunden</b>'s grand love-story. <br><br>A yummy breathtaking lovely biker MAN...<br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/image.jpg3_zpseu1qf8sh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432608077i/14987802.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg3_zpseu1qf8sh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>‘He was leaning back against the steps, his hands linked across his chest, his legs outstretched and crossed at the ankles. Damn, he was big. And not hard at all to look at. <br><br>Well-worn black engineer boots. Dark straight-leg Levis. Black button-down shirt, folded back on his arms and open at the throat. Leather cuffs. Leather kutte. Black Ray-Bans. He looked like Mr. June in the Harley Biker Beefcake calendar.’</blockquote><br>...some hot, steamy but so very tender love...<br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Couple%20in%20love/image.jpg1_zpscouzei6p.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432485014i/14970636.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg1_zpscouzei6p.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br>...and a tough incredible heroine Woman. <br><br>*********************************************************<br><br><b>What to say? Why...?!?</b><br>First of all: this novel has a intriguing storyline, a interesting topic and a great thrilling plot. You don't get "it" all to start with. You have to wait, discover and get piece by piece. In some ways predictable (the romance) in other not at all (the plot and twists). <br><br><b>Maybe not intense but kind of moldering emotional</b>. <br>It's hard to say why but this story felt slightly different (compared with many other m/f CR) with it's own style, way of telling. Quietly dramatic without being overly melodramatic (thanks for that!!). No what ever to be compared to any silly cheesy romances stuff. Instead a bit rough and thrilling exiting.<br><br>Best of all (you have all heard me nagging about it over and over before..): I'm not a young girl myself and I ADORE those great contemporary romances with mature grownup adult characters - like in this one (~ 33 and 38). ~ Thanks for that! ~ I always want my sweet heart wrenching stuff too, and this is rough and raw in parts but also so very awesome romantic and freaking intense HOT. You could feel their connection. <br><blockquote>
<a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/image.jpg3_zpseu1qf8sh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432608077i/14987802.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg3_zpseu1qf8sh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>‘She wanted it rough; she always wanted it rough. But Isaac found that he was too overwhelmed by love and too haunted by the fear of losing her to be anything but sweet right now, to this woman who’d found a place in his heart he hadn’t known was there. He kissed her, holding her close, his hands all over her, but gently, soothing.’<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Couple%20in%20love/c6ae26df-5b42-4a6e-9b7b-2a62f0938ae6_zpsiiznm7yy.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433045024i/15042865.jpg" alt=" photo c6ae26df-5b42-4a6e-9b7b-2a62f0938ae6_zpsiiznm7yy.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br><b>Lilli: A mysterious heroine to admire</b>. So far from an damsel in distress a romance heroine could be. It was good to wonder most about the heroine instead of the other way around. She is a anmazing, but shadowy character it took time to get a grip on. She both has a high independence and strong self-confidence about herself and her desires. ~ Lilli (Sport) is doubtless the kind of interesting heroine I like to meet more often. <br><br><b>Isaac: A tough guy but also the most tender and lovely</b> biker man you can imagine. I loved, LOVED, this yummy wonderful man from the very first page. ~ Isaac is the kind of manly sexy MAN hero I prefer (need, want, love..) in m/f romances. <br><blockquote>‘No. Not one way or another. .(..). He never thought to have this; he never thought he wanted it. But he had it, this love, this <i>binding</i> with another soul, and he was not giving it up. Fuck no. ...’<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Diverse/image.jpg3_zpseu1qf8sh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432608077i/14987802.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg3_zpseu1qf8sh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br><b>A thrilling, gripping story... for me. Yay!</b><br>Just a wonderful good m/f read. This will be a great adventure to continue. We didn't get a annoying unfair cliffy here —we have them in a quite nice place— but life (or the all over plot) isn't solved. I just NEED to really soon get to know what's up next for the <i>'Night Horde'</i> boys and these unforgettable lovebirds. ~ <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><br>Already damaging my beautiful pink nails... — I'm afraid it will be heartbreaking nasty. I fear life in Signal Bend isn't a easy piece of cake. Or?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>********************************************************* <br><br><b>I LIKE - ...happy dancing book-LOVE moments</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4992310440109578275"><b>4.5 MC, Love, Saviors & Duty Stars<br/><br/><i>"L' amor che muove il sole e l'altre stelle."</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392303748i/8535433.jpg' width='400' height='224' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>In the sleepy town of <i>Signal Bend</i> nothing really changes...<br/><br/><b>Isaac</b> as the president of the Night Horde MC has a duty towards his brothers and his town. Serve and protect. Uphold the law, defend and make whatever he has, illegal or not to keep them safe and well. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431991i/867222._SX540_.gif' width='400' height='224' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>An honorable man, a talented artist, a biker that doesn't afraid. He knows violence and he does what needs to be done. Until a stranger in his town will threa</span>
  <span id="freeText4992310440109578275" style="display:none"><b>4.5 MC, Love, Saviors &amp; Duty Stars<br><br><i>"L' amor che muove il sole e l'altre stelle."</i></b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392303748i/8535433.jpg" width="400" height="224" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>In the sleepy town of <i>Signal Bend</i> nothing really changes...<br><br><b>Isaac</b> as the president of the Night Horde MC has a duty towards his brothers and his town. Serve and protect. Uphold the law, defend and make whatever he has, illegal or not to keep them safe and well. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431991i/867222._SX540_.gif" width="400" height="224" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>An honorable man, a talented artist, a biker that doesn't afraid. He knows violence and he does what needs to be done. Until a stranger in his town will threaten the bonds between the brotherhood and his heart.<br><br><b>Lilli</b> is a woman of many secrets, layers and nightmares. Familiar with tragedy a true loner with a strong sense of honor and duty. Lethal and tormented, she needs vengeance to claim the peace that eludes her. Coming to town seemed easy but she wasn't expecting a biker to stand with her and steal her heart. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390601774i/8249895.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Together will set the sheets on fire and come to realise that will have to fight together and make a stand against what threatens them. Now, if they only manage to survive it...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392303748i/8535434.jpg" width="400" height="180" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Holy cow.... That was awesome! Sexy, dangerous, mysterious, it hooked right from the heartbreaking prologue right until the promising finale. It reminded me of the good ol' Linda Howard books that I used to devour back in my late teens, with a biker twist. Strong, determined heroine; awesome, powerful hero with a huge dash of steam and love.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429862i/861536.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Move the Sun</i> is an intriguing story that keeps you on your toes and steals a piece of your heart. Well-adjusted characters, multi-layered plot, it's kinda unique and easy to read. Suspenseful and so damn sexy, it won't disappoint you and you will become invested in Isaac &amp; Lilli's relationship and if you are a bit like me you will start the next immediately!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/670118.gif" width="400" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_922910423" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/922910423" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/922910423?book_show_action=true">Apr 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=best-of-2014">best-of-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer922910423" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer921620412913737903"><b>5 ultimate biker book STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410044521i/11056413.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Move the Sun was utterly perfect and I'm in awe. I know what you think...not another biker book, but I swear this one is different. Seriously! <br/>The latest conquest on my biker-book-bender was a full on surprise, a success and downright amazeballs. You don't get those very often.<br/><br/>When I first read the blurb my head went all damsel in distress, on the run from the big evil and hell...I couldn't have been more wrong if I'd tried. It's not like the others and I'm so grateful</span>
  <span id="freeText921620412913737903" style="display:none"><b>5 ultimate biker book STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410044521i/11056413.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Move the Sun was utterly perfect and I'm in awe. I know what you think...not another biker book, but I swear this one is different. Seriously! <br>The latest conquest on my biker-book-bender was a full on surprise, a success and downright amazeballs. You don't get those very often.<br><br>When I first read the blurb my head went all damsel in distress, on the run from the big evil and hell...I couldn't have been more wrong if I'd tried. It's not like the others and I'm so grateful that I finally gave it a try.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>”L'amor che muove il sole e l'altre stelle.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This is the story of Lilli and Isaac. She is the mysterious new girl, who right away catches the eyes of the local bad boy and leader of the Motorcycle Club. <br>You see, Signal Bend is in the middle of nowhere, people don't move in...they usually just run of there. So it isn't strange that the pretty dark haired lady, with a proclivity for too short running attire raises eyebrows and most definitely warrants a check-up ...really a full body search... by one very curious biker.<br><br>Simple enough, right? Ahhhh, but this one has a twist and I'm not going to tell you what it is, but it is highly entertaining and sexy and pretty original as far as biker book plots go. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>”I don’t know any other woman like you—as strong as you, or as smart. You make me stronger. It’s when we’re not working together that we’re weaker. We make a good team. We fill each other out. We fit. I feel that. Do you?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Lilli Accardo</b> is an amazing character and heroin. She is cool, calculated, not much can shock her and she is as far from a naïve little girl as one could possibly get. But that's just window dressing; she has secrets, big secrets and I was biting my nails trying to figure it all out. <br><br>And of course while keeping all those secrets and playing all mysterious and such, a girl can always dabble in a little 'something' with a gorgeous man.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410109957ra/11063127.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I especially liked how Ms. Fanetti neatly wove in some flashbacks to create a bigger picture for us to see what happened in Lilli's past and what ultimately lead her to this town. It's not a coincidence that she is here and you bet your ass that woman has an ulterior motive.<br><br>Also, the same day Lilli appears in Signal Bend trouble within the community and the clubs business dealings arises. Coincidence? Well, who knows? Curious? Most definitely.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>”Well-worn black engineer boots. Dark straight-leg Levis. Black button-down shirt, folded back on his arms and open at the throat. Leather cuffs. Leather kutte. Black Ray-Bans. He looked like Mr. June in the Harley biker Beefcake calendar.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Isaac Lunden</b> is the president of Night Horde MC Club. For Signal Bend he is the law and order, without him and his club there wouldn't be a town left. Signal Bend is for all intents and purposes a dead town and the only things that keep the lights on are the illegal dealings of the Horde. He loves his town and his people and he will do just about anything to protect them.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400108393ra/9636054.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yup, he has a lot on his plate and when Lilli walks into his town he is highly suspicious and well...horny, really. Ever since their first meeting these two have some insane chemistry and they are very much in tune with each other, even though they can't explain why.<br><br>Suffice it to say that Lilli is Isaac’s match in every sense of the word. She is one tough cookie and these two strong willed characters don't do anything halfway. They even challenge each other in bed, bargaining for their pleasure and it's the most fun I've had reading in while.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>”They'd literally fought their way to a fuck.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411409ra/807961.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Mmmmmh, Lilli and Isaac are a pretty fun couple. They don't do bullshit. They both know what they want and they take it. No questions asked...deal with truth and consequences later if you will.<br><br>But beside the obvious relationship storyline, Ms. F. created a very rich world with real characters and interesting history, a very complex world and a well thought out plot. <br><br>I'd recommend this book to anyone who likes a non-annoying kick-ass heroine, hotter than hell biker shenanigans, sweet romance and occasionally a rough ride. Pun most definitely intended!<br><br>Can't wait to read the next one!<br><br><br><i>**Thanks for the fabulous BR, Suzanne and Stephanie!! ;D</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
