<div id="review_846493557" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/846493557" />
    <a title="♥Sharon♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12125670-sharon"><img alt="♥Sharon♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417537732p2/12125670.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/846493557?book_show_action=true">Feb 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Sharon♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Sharon♥" href="/user/show/12125670-sharon">♥Sharon♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer846493557" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8723411288274080484">I ❤ Isaac<br/>I ❤ Lilli<br/><br/>I really haven’t read all that many MC books but something about this series caught my eye. I read a few review for Move the Sun and others within this series and though there appears to be some grittiness about them, they also had a bit of a different vibe to them. <br/><br/><a href='http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/Movethesun_zps1a4af6eb.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397756701i/9323300._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo Movethesun_zps1a4af6eb.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Move the Sun was an amazing story. It was lsaac and Lilli’s story and I LOVED it. <br/><br/>Lilli shows up in Signal Bend, Missouri. Being a stranger in town, she catches the eye of just about everyone, including Isaac wh</span>
  <span id="freeText8723411288274080484" style="display:none">I ❤ Isaac<br>I ❤ Lilli<br><br>I really haven’t read all that many MC books but something about this series caught my eye. I read a few review for Move the Sun and others within this series and though there appears to be some grittiness about them, they also had a bit of a different vibe to them. <br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/Movethesun_zps1a4af6eb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397756701i/9323300._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Movethesun_zps1a4af6eb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Move the Sun was an amazing story. It was lsaac and Lilli’s story and I LOVED it. <br><br>Lilli shows up in Signal Bend, Missouri. Being a stranger in town, she catches the eye of just about everyone, including Isaac who is the President of the local Motorcycle Club. Lilli has her reasons for being in town, ones that she keeps to herself. Lilli is a lot of things. She is beautiful and sexy. She is also very strong willed and independent. <br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/lillimovethesun_zpsd2d20816.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397756701i/9323301._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo lillimovethesun_zpsd2d20816.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Isaac was more than just your badass biker. He was a protector. Seeing Lilli stirred something within him that he wasn’t expecting. The attraction was instant. He knew what he wanted with Lilli but he also knew Lilli had secrets. <br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/IsaacMovetheSun_zpsb863dda1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397756701i/9323302.jpg" alt=" photo IsaacMovetheSun_zpsb863dda1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>What unfolds between these two was sexy and hot as hell. Isaac and Lilli just fit perfectly together. Their desires for each other were intense. Each giving the other exactly what they needed.<br><br>❤Under the Oak Tree❤<br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/oaktreemovethesun_zpsf6a55957.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397756701i/9323303.jpg" alt=" photo oaktreemovethesun_zpsf6a55957.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“Ah, Christ. Do you know how fucking good you feel on me? So damn tight and soft, holding me in. I love the way you smell, the way you taste. I love the sounds you make. Fuck, baby, I love you.”</i>
</b><br><br>As Lilli’s secrets come to the surface and other things within the MC comes to a head things start to get intense for everyone. Watching Isaac instinctively protect Lilli made my heart do funny things and I loved watching Lilli slowly give pieces of herself to Isaac. <br> <br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/lilliandisaac_zps5ecf4b82.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397756701i/9323304.jpg" alt=" photo lilliandisaac_zps5ecf4b82.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“I really love you, Sport. You’re it for me. You fill up a space in me I didn’t even know was empty.”</i>
</b><br><br>If you love MC books you will absolutely love Move the Sun and I would have to assume the rest of this series! <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8723411288274080484" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="S.M. West" class="user" itemprop="url" name="S.M. West" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west">S.M. West</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer850212512" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17489912466986858080"><b> 5 ASTOUNDING STARS</b><br/><br/>I love biker stories and yes, like many of you, I’ve read A LOT of MC stories. But, I gotta say, I’m putting this book among the top of the heap. <br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/bHKHCcQ' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410149396ra/11067592.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>It was a captivating read. I've read other really good biker books and while I was riveted and loving it, I felt like I was watching it all unfold through the window; I wasn't in the thick of it. Not this book. IMO, Ms. Fanetti's writing style draws you in. I felt like this was my story, like I was there in Signal Bend. And Lilli</span>
  <span id="freeText17489912466986858080" style="display:none"><b> 5 ASTOUNDING STARS</b><br><br>I love biker stories and yes, like many of you, I’ve read A LOT of MC stories. But, I gotta say, I’m putting this book among the top of the heap. <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/bHKHCcQ" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410149396ra/11067592.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It was a captivating read. I've read other really good biker books and while I was riveted and loving it, I felt like I was watching it all unfold through the window; I wasn't in the thick of it. Not this book. IMO, Ms. Fanetti's writing style draws you in. I felt like this was my story, like I was there in Signal Bend. And Lilli, Isaac and the others, were my people. <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/MTS_zps85f40663.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410232666i/11077839._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo MTS_zps85f40663.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>LILLI ACCARDO <br><br><i>“She was something special, something to behold. Something dangerous.”</i></b><br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/28168_serinda-swan-estrena-primer-episodio-breakout-kings_zps950c209f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410149396i/11067593._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 28168_serinda-swan-estrena-primer-episodio-breakout-kings_zps950c209f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lilli is an amazing heroine!! There are very few like her. Susan Fanetti creates wonderfully, amazing female characters that kick-ass!! Lilli is smart, brave, strong and knows what she wants and knows just how to get it.<br><br><b>ISAAC LUNDEN<br><br><i>“Fuck, the man was all elemental sex.”</i></b><br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/MovetheSun_zps70a4dea6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410149987i/11067636._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo MovetheSun_zps70a4dea6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Isaac is unlike any other MC president I've read and I freakin' LOVE him!!<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/baoQX4C" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410149396ra/11067595.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And together...Lilli and Isaac have this wild, unbridled, lasting passion.<br><br><b>“I’m not gonna fuck you, baby. I’m gonna move you. Let me. Let me have you.”</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/1rethOp" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410149396ra/11067596.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br><b>“I love you, Sport. You’re it for me. You fill up a space in me I didn’t even know was empty.”</b> <br><br>If you like Motorcycle Club stories, kick-ass heroines and hot as f*&amp;k Alpha males, <b>READ THIS BOOK.</b><br><br>This was a Buddy Read with Flo and Stephanie. Thanks girls for joining me on the ride! </span>

    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/850119805?book_show_action=true">Feb 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Susan Fanetti Fans, Biker genre, Strong Women, Romance</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer850119805" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15390715778461385819"><b>
  <i>This was the book that started my love affair with Susan Fanetti. Friends on GR were talking about this amazing new writer and since I valued their opinion, I hopped on board. This series came at a time when MC Clubs were very strong in pop culture, think Sons of Anarchy. Only this series ran much deeper and hit places in the readers more personally. This wasn't a series to take lightly, we never could see what was coming. There were times of amazing joy and times that ripped your heart out c</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText15390715778461385819" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>This was the book that started my love affair with Susan Fanetti. Friends on GR were talking about this amazing new writer and since I valued their opinion, I hopped on board. This series came at a time when MC Clubs were very strong in pop culture, think Sons of Anarchy. Only this series ran much deeper and hit places in the readers more personally. This wasn't a series to take lightly, we never could see what was coming. There were times of amazing joy and times that ripped your heart out causing readers to decide whether to continue. All I can personally say is it was worth it to me and I have been a devoted fan of Ms. Fanetti's writing ever since. </i>
</b><br><br><b>4.5 Disturbing, Incredibly Strong, Character-Driven Stars <br>* * * * 1/2<br>In my life, the only contact I have ever had with bikers has been either just seeing them on the road or through film or television. In 2008 a show came on cable... it was raunchy, full of drama, yes... lots of eye candy... but also had real character development and plot. It was Sons of Anarchy. That show was my personal experience... until I started reading all of the MC books that have been out. <br><br>I have to say my education has been thorough. I have read all types from Biker Lite to Hardcore. All of the books have given me different concepts of this life; people with the unifying love of freedom and making rules which are held, dear. There are core principals; break these rules and people will pay. The men are strong, Alpha and sometimes have an actual love for their women which develops into a life-changing event.<br><br>Move the Sun (Signal Bend#1) by Susan Fanetti </b> was a very special read for me. I knew it was about bikers... but this felt personal. It felt like the author had a real stake in it... like she was telling her life...somehow, at least to me. It had the feel of what has taken place in America; parts of our country becoming more and more isolated due to no employment or industries to support the community. The question is what is the remedy for these people... what does a town do to survive...<br><br>This book addresses this perfectly and gives us an understanding of why and how this all happens. But this part of the story provides the background for the real story... the real draw for this book. This book has provided us with an Epic couple... we get the love story of Issac and Lilli.<br><br>These two characters, in my opinion, happen to be the most perfectly matched. Both have had life experiences that have groomed them for each other. Issac ... all Alpha, Bearded, huge in stature and has the responsibilities of the town and club placed firmly on his shoulders. His outside maybe be rough but his heart is caring.<br><br>Lilli is a woman with strength, purpose and focus beyond compare. She is one of a kind. It is worth reading this book and series just to meet her.<br><br>To tell you more about her would take away from your read... <br><br>This is a series that needs to read if you have any interest in the biker life. It is not a diluted version; it is gritty, raw and off-color. But it also is humane... there are moments of great sweetness.... like in real life..by people who are not sweet or nice...I just felt all of it rang true and not forced.<br><br>This is only the beginning... and if the level of excellence stays the same... then I promise, you will not be disappointed. I know I haven't been. <br> <br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19235985.Move_the_Sun__Signal_Bend___1_" title="Move the Sun (Signal Bend, #1) by Susan Fanetti" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1386343963l/19235985._SX50_.jpg" alt="Move the Sun (Signal Bend, #1) by Susan Fanetti" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer844705276" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13325072624330215747"><b>******10+++ Badass Stars******</b><br/><br/><b>MUST READ!!! MUST READ!!! MUST READ!!! MUST READ!!!</b><br/><br/>I'm a total fan of Motorcycle Club stories; anything I can read, watch and research about the MC lifestyle, I'm all over it... I really mean no disrespect or comparison to other MC books but <i>Move The Sun</i> might be the best one I've ever read in this genre. This book was brilliantly written, the plot was gripping from beginning to end and the characters were strong and compelling. I can't wait to continue reading, goo</span>
  <span id="freeText13325072624330215747" style="display:none"><b>******10+++ Badass Stars******</b><br><br><b>MUST READ!!! MUST READ!!! MUST READ!!! MUST READ!!!</b><br><br>I'm a total fan of Motorcycle Club stories; anything I can read, watch and research about the MC lifestyle, I'm all over it... I really mean no disrespect or comparison to other MC books but <i>Move The Sun</i> might be the best one I've ever read in this genre. This book was brilliantly written, the plot was gripping from beginning to end and the characters were strong and compelling. I can't wait to continue reading, good news for me, there's four more books in this series.<br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/c4d6ed25-3566-4a6c-bc7f-169628b6d0ab_zps5edbbbdc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397234869i/9251835.jpg" alt=" photo c4d6ed25-3566-4a6c-bc7f-169628b6d0ab_zps5edbbbdc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lilli Accardo is the mysterious new woman in town; the day she arrives in the town of Signal Bend she encounters the dangerous Isaac Lunden, president of the Night Horde MC. Lilli is badass and she is far from scared of him, turn on is more what she's feeling towards the man. Isaac and Lillie don't waste time playing games and they are both people who take what they want; and after an explosive night together they simply cant get enough. But there's a lot of secrets hiding, and Isaac's priority is his club and his people, for Lillie is her mission; a personal vendetta that has become her life purpose. Will their interests collide and put them against each other? or will they own up to to the intensity of their feelings and fight the world in order to stay together? <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/0d5ebac2-2ce5-4368-a5ca-8c7ae62730a6_zpsfc5f2c23.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397234869i/9251836._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 0d5ebac2-2ce5-4368-a5ca-8c7ae62730a6_zpsfc5f2c23.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I must be blunt and admit that I have a girl crush on Lilli, she's got to be one the coolest, most clever female character I've read about in a book. While there was angst in the story, it was never over dramatic and this chick handled herself in such an mazing way, every single time. She was successful in more than one way but also humble about it, and I love strong female characters that don't take BS from anybody, Loved her!!<br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/5dcd9651-367f-4053-b02f-21c0d996f1e3_zps6c7f6437.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1397234869i/9251837._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 5dcd9651-367f-4053-b02f-21c0d996f1e3_zps6c7f6437.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Absolutely terrific novel, brilliantly written. I'm totally hooked! Do yourself a favor and go pick up this book, you will regret not having read it already.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13325072624330215747" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer299997151668737363">I really enjoyed this one. Lilli was a badass lead and Isaac was a drool worthy MC biker. And boy could these two throw down in the bedroom. Throw DOWN. <br/><br/>It was also refreshing to read about a MC biker GANG that actually acts like a GANG. I mean, don't get me wrong, I love me some Kristen Ashley Chaos action, but let's get real people - Tack's MC is a little more rainbows and unicorns and a little less reality. Now I am totally down with pots of gold and mythically horned horse, however, it's als</span>
  <span id="freeText299997151668737363" style="display:none">I really enjoyed this one. Lilli was a badass lead and Isaac was a drool worthy MC biker. And boy could these two throw down in the bedroom. Throw DOWN. <br /><br />It was also refreshing to read about a MC biker GANG that actually acts like a GANG. I mean, don't get me wrong, I love me some Kristen Ashley Chaos action, but let's get real people - Tack's MC is a little more rainbows and unicorns and a little less reality. Now I am totally down with pots of gold and mythically horned horse, however, it's also nice to get a little authenticity now and again. <br /><br />Isaac and his boys drink, smoke weed, and fuck people up. Bring. It. On.<br /><br />Definitely looking forward to book two. <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5562009919760754802"><b> *** 3 STARS***</b> <br/><br/> I liked <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19235985.Move_the_Sun__Signal_Bend___1_' title='Move the Sun (Signal Bend, #1) by Susan Fanetti' rel='nofollow noopener'>Move the Sun</a> but I didn't love it...<br/><br/>Wait, wait, wait, before your start rolling your eyes at me please <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400133341ra/9639400.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/>Some readers have an aversion to inaccurate language translation,while others loath cultural misconceptions.   <span id="freeText5562009919760754802" style="display:none"><b> *** 3 STARS***</b> <br><br> I liked <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19235985.Move_the_Sun__Signal_Bend___1_" title="Move the Sun (Signal Bend, #1) by Susan Fanetti" rel="nofollow noopener">Move the Sun</a> but I didn't love it...<br><br>Wait, wait, wait, before your start rolling your eyes at me please <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400133341ra/9639400.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Some readers have an aversion to inaccurate language translation,while others loath cultural misconceptions. Shit, pilots would never lead any type of Command Investigation, PERIOD. That's what military investigators are for.... service members attend extensive military schooling/training, it's an actual MOS/RATE aka.JOB. <br><br>* I'm 99% certain that w/Lilli's rank and job performance the army would not have discharged her. <br><br>*Lilli works for NSA- as in <b> NATIONAL </b> Security Agency --&gt; Huh?... I'm just going to need you to trust me when I say NSA DOES NOT perform Top Secret (personal) Vendetta Missions. <br><br>*Lilli spilled way too much information, way too easily..sorry but if you work for NSA you know better. <br><br>* NSA contractor get paid $$$$$ .. I have a really hard time believing her co-worker would be willing to help the meth trafficking motorcycle club with their turf war... Yeah, that shit would get him fired in a heart beat.. I'm curios to see if Lilli still works for the NSA as being engaged to said meth smuggling MC president is a conflict of interest. <br><br>*Channels of communicating TSI are DIFFERENT then the norm. <br><br>*Also, Issac's constant growling during sex and Lilli's weird hair obsession --&gt; she was constantly pulling the rubber band from his ponytail (I kept imaging Jason Momoa in a Pantene Ad) irked me a <s>lot </s>incy wincy bit.......I KNOW, I'm a ROYAL pain in the ass..... I own it . <br><br>* thank you, my list is complete. :-) <br>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br>....okay, you may roll your eyes to your hearts content. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393822544i/8769144._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, I would like to take a moment to say <b> THANK YOU </b> to Susan Fanetti for writing one Fan-Fucking -Tastc heroine. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400142632ra/9640429.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> ......it's true. I appreciate the fact that he wasn't your typical uber alpha motor mouth club president . He gets my seal of approval.....but Showdown gets everything else ...yup, I don't know what it is with me and supporting characters but I'm team Showdown.....for now :-) <br><br><b> For more reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394322574i/8836468._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer851945888" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7559413947564592397">4.5 This Moved my Sun Stars!<br/><br/>This little gem sat unread on my kindle forever...dummy me! What a fabulous start to what seems to be a great series.<br/><br/>Lilli "Carson" is tough. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572238i/11813533._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>She is mysterious beauty who has taken residence in Signal Bend. She has no one, nothing...perhaps this is just a new start.<br/><br/>Isaac Lundan knows "his town." He knows everyone in his town. He knows everyone's business in town.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572238i/11813534._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Now there is this strange beauty that has piqued his interest both mentally and physically. Like any other </span>
  <span id="freeText7559413947564592397" style="display:none">4.5 This Moved my Sun Stars!<br><br>This little gem sat unread on my kindle forever...dummy me! What a fabulous start to what seems to be a great series.<br><br>Lilli "Carson" is tough. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572238i/11813533._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She is mysterious beauty who has taken residence in Signal Bend. She has no one, nothing...perhaps this is just a new start.<br><br>Isaac Lundan knows "his town." He knows everyone in his town. He knows everyone's business in town.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572238i/11813534._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now there is this strange beauty that has piqued his interest both mentally and physically. Like any other tough talking, bad ass acting MC prez...he stakes a claim.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572238i/11813535._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their connection is immediate. Lilli plays no games. She may have her hidden secrets and her own agenda, but he she wants the danger and the intimacy that this bad boy is offering! Oh, and what he offers, and what she takes is beyond amazing!<br><br>What happens with Lilli and Isaac is raw, primal, and yet beautiful. Both have secrets, both have issues, but one thing is for sure, they have found an unlikely partnership with one another. They have found a comfort and real connection...a need to "be" with someone for the first time in ages.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415572238i/11813536.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love this story. I love the sensuality and the erotic nature of their relationship. I loved the mystery and the hidden danger and violence. What I loved the most though, is the way this author made the big and bad fall in love without losing the "big and the bad." Reading Isaac and Lilli's progression was amazing. The chemistry was hot, the communication was open and honest, and the overall future looks promising. Somehow, I don't think it will be HEA just yet!!!</span>

<div id="review_840378753" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/840378753" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/840378753?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=biker-romance">biker-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=damaged-hero-heroine">damaged-hero-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=military-war">military-war</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=buddy-read-with-steph">buddy-read-with-steph</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=may-reads">may-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer840378753" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer798841559776553798">I absolutely LOVED this book! It has been some time since a book has captured my whole focus from the first page; but this one did that from start to finish! The prologue was intense, and from then I knew I was hooked! "Move the Sun" has got to be one of my top fave MC books out there. Yes, it is dark at times; but not to the point where it over powers the whole book. There is just as much romance, but it isn't your "la-dee-da" flowery kind of romance..It is the primal, hot, and animalistic kind</span>
  <span id="freeText798841559776553798" style="display:none">I absolutely LOVED this book! It has been some time since a book has captured my whole focus from the first page; but this one did that from start to finish! The prologue was intense, and from then I knew I was hooked! "Move the Sun" has got to be one of my top fave MC books out there. Yes, it is dark at times; but not to the point where it over powers the whole book. There is just as much romance, but it isn't your "la-dee-da" flowery kind of romance..It is the primal, hot, and animalistic kind; basically what you would expect from the president of the Motor Cycle club and a woman who is hard core mainly due from her life experiences. This was the first time I had read a Susan Fanetti book, but I will add that this woman knows how to write. I am now officially her reading slave! I will read whatever she writes, and I can't wait to dig into the rest of this Signal Bend series!!<br /><br />Lilli Accardo is hands down my most favorite heroine out of most of the stories I have read..and that is saying something because I have read thousands of books! This woman is a badass, and she arrives in the town of Signal Bend,Missouri with secrets. She catches the eye of the President of the Night Horde MC; Isaac Lunden immediately when she drives through town in a car that most men drool over! Isaac wastes no time in approaching her, and very quickly he picks up on the vibe that she is surrounded in mystery. He needs to figure out whether or not she is a threat to his club or town, and he decides if she is..then she is going down. Unfortunately though, he wants her in a bad way, and so he takes her; and let me tell you; when these two come together, it is nothing short of a major explosion. These two give angry,primal,animalistic sex a new definition! Holy hell, when they get it on, there is nothing that can pull me away from my Kindle! Wowsa, these two know how to burn up the sheets, and then the next day they are counting their many bruises and scratches, and wondering why they are both limping! I LOVED it! Actually, every scene with the couple in it was awesome. I love them together. My favorite thing about them is how honest they are with one another, and they put all their cards on the table and don't mess around. It is a refreshing change to see the main couple not throwing out all of the drama because they are cheating on each other or bickering. Lilli and Isaac both know what they want and they grab it and hang on with both hands. The only drama in this story is from outside forces, and believe me; it keeps them all on their toes.<br /><br />All in all, this is a must read for anyone who loves a great biker series! This is going down as my favorite, and move over Sons of Anarchy; there is a new club in town..and they are known as "The Night Horde." I have decided to head right into the next book and get back to Isaac and Lilli to see what else they are up against..One thing is for sure..as long as they have each other; they will remain unstoppable!!! Ms. Fanetti, you are brilliant; and I can't wait to discover what else you have in store for the town of Signal Bend!<br /><br />Just need to add a thank you to my Buddy Reading partner Steph! I am so glad you joined me in reading this series! Also, happy to have Nicole and Shanna join in too! The more the merrier, oh..and I think Daisy also joined us as well! Great series, and even better Buddies to have to read it with!♥</span>
  <a data-text-id="798841559776553798" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2834326223145640225"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399157298i/9516316._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='411' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Move the Sun</i> was a well written, original, hot, biker story. I did struggle a little in the beginning, but once the story got going I really enjoyed it.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"L' amor che muove il sole e l'altre stelle."</i>
</b><br/><br/>The story starts with Lilli arriving in Signal Bend, where she catches the eye of Issac, president of the Night Horde MC club. Lilli is such a kickass heroine. She is tough, honest, and focused. I really liked her. She and Issac share an intense sexual attraction from the start and begin seeing eac</span>
  <span id="freeText2834326223145640225" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399157298i/9516316._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="411" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Move the Sun</i> was a well written, original, hot, biker story. I did struggle a little in the beginning, but once the story got going I really enjoyed it.<br><br><b>
  <i>"L' amor che muove il sole e l'altre stelle."</i>
</b><br><br>The story starts with Lilli arriving in Signal Bend, where she catches the eye of Issac, president of the Night Horde MC club. Lilli is such a kickass heroine. She is tough, honest, and focused. I really liked her. She and Issac share an intense sexual attraction from the start and begin seeing each other. Meaning, lots of rough, hot sex.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399158523i/9516433.png" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But things are complicated for both Lilli and Issac. What is the real reason for Lilli's arrival in Signal Bend and will Issac stand in her way? Issac is dedicated to his club and town, but Lilli awakens feelings he didn't know he had. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I love you, Sport. You’re it for me. You fill up a space in me I didn’t even know was empty.”</i>
</b> <br><br>So both characters find themselves in difficult situations. As things heat up fast and feelings grow. Lilli and Issac find themselves torn, in the end where will their loyalties lie?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399158232i/9516410._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This one is pretty steamy, Lilli and Issac are off the charts hot. I liked having both Lilli and Issac's POV. There is a bit of insta-love/lust, but I still found the relationship building compelling and didn't take away from the story. I am looking forward to seeing how the series progresses.</span>

<div id="review_1263596740" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1263596740" />
    <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog"><img alt="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420222674p2/38657470.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1263596740?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)" href="/user/show/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog">Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Angela (Reading Frenzy Book Blog) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=xanax-alert">xanax-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-fav-series">book-1-of-fav-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=its-getting-hot-in-here">its-getting-hot-in-here</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/38657470-angela-reading-frenzy-book-blog?shelf=military">military</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1263596740" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10345802455598040675">I take it back; I like biker books after all. I’ve heard Susan Fanetti’s praises sung over and over so I was eager to read one of her books. Amy (Foxy) suggested I start with this one but I don’t consider myself to be a fan of MC books so I was braced for disappointment. Well butter my butt and call me a biscuit! I enjoyed the heck out of this novel.<br/><br/>I honestly think it’s best if you read this book knowing nothing other than what you read in the book blurb. I will say that the story alternates be</span>
  <span id="freeText10345802455598040675" style="display:none">I take it back; I like biker books after all. I’ve heard Susan Fanetti’s praises sung over and over so I was eager to read one of her books. Amy (Foxy) suggested I start with this one but I don’t consider myself to be a fan of MC books so I was braced for disappointment. Well butter my butt and call me a biscuit! I enjoyed the heck out of this novel.<br><br>I honestly think it’s best if you read this book knowing nothing other than what you read in the book blurb. I will say that the story alternates between the present and the protagonist's past. I think I enjoyed the process of discovering Lilli’s motivations more because I went into it blind. I’m one of those pesky readers who can frequently predict the path a plot will take and accurately guess the stupid things a character is about to do. I can see a plot twist coming a mile away and figure out whodunit long before the detectives solve the case. The fact that Lilli’s backstory and intentions weren’t obvious to me is a testament to Susan Fanetti’s writing skills and execution. She also took the sting out my objections to any given character’s actions by addressing them immediately after I raised them. Mad skills I tell you!<br><br>Lilli Accardo in three words: <b>focused, sexy, badass</b>. She is, hands down, one of my top five favorite book heroines. There isn’t an ounce of deception in her character. Yes, she is secretive; however, she refuses to lie which makes her a woman of integrity. Lilli is determined and scary smart. She knows what she wants—in bed and in life—and she doesn’t ask for it or even demand it; she just takes it. She’s tough and maybe too hardened but I like her. I want to be her when I grow up.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436730346i/15496963.jpg" alt=" photo Lilli_zpsyth9jcgc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Isaac Lunden in three words: <b>dependable, sexy, badass</b>. Wait. Did I just describe Lilli? No, but they’re perfect for each other. Isaac is a stereotypical biker dude in many ways. He’s got that whole leather jacket, beard, long hair, outlaw, tough guy thing working for him. He’s also warm, funny, honest, and extremely sensitive. Isaac asking Lilli to talk to him about her feelings took me by surprise yet seems perfectly natural.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436730346i/15496964._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Isaac4_zpsyeutw1kk.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lilli and Isaac together? Can you say, “spontaneous combustion”? These two have hot and dirty sex all over Signal Bend: on the floor, in a public restroom, against the wall, under a tree, in an office, in a lake, on a yoga mat. You get the picture. There’s definitely insta-lust here which normally bugs me but for some reason it works. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436730423ra/15496969.gif" alt=" photo Fanvajay_zpscan38zzm.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love that in the middle of all the action, suspense, and sexy times there are many moments of humor between the pair. <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Who even came up with a stupid word like falafel? Sounds like a frog with tonsillitis.”<br><br>“It’s Middle Eastern, and you are a being a big baby. At least try it. I promise you won’t turn into a vegetarian if one meal you eat in your life doesn’t have an animal in it.”<br><br>He pulled his plate back. “Yeah, something tells me this is a gateway sandwich.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>Consider me a Fanetti fan. I didn’t have to think twice about rating this book five stars. Isaac and Lilli’s story continues in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19266169.Behold_the_Stars__Signal_Bend___2_" title="Behold the Stars (Signal Bend, #2) by Susan Fanetti" rel="nofollow noopener">Behold the Stars</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10345802455598040675" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer832314600" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3758002299363059227">2020, May - another read of one of my all time favorite series. Just to go back and remember; to hurt and feel and love through these amazing characters. <br/><br/>2017 re-read of the series. Isaac and Lilli are just as amazing as I remember. So many things to remember. Even more learning all over again the beauty of this group. In love. <br/><br/><b>5++++ <i>"Something dangerous."</i> Stars</b><br/><br/><i>Move the Sun</i> chronicles the journey of Lilli Accardo and Night Horde MC President Isaac Lunden. It’s an awesome MC story. I’ve become a </span>
  <span id="freeText3758002299363059227" style="display:none">2020, May - another read of one of my all time favorite series. Just to go back and remember; to hurt and feel and love through these amazing characters. <br /><br />2017 re-read of the series. Isaac and Lilli are just as amazing as I remember. So many things to remember. Even more learning all over again the beauty of this group. In love. <br /><br /><b>5++++ <i>"Something dangerous."</i> Stars</b><br /><br /><i>Move the Sun</i> chronicles the journey of Lilli Accardo and Night Horde MC President Isaac Lunden. It’s an awesome MC story. I’ve become a total Susan Fanetti fangirl. Recommended to me by a GR friend, I started Move the Sun with no expectations of what I’d find in Signal Bend, a small town hanging on by a thread held by the local MC. Any expectations I may have had would be blown right out the water. Fanetti’s descriptive writing allows us to feel like we’ve teleported right to the heart of Missouri in the dying small town of Signal Bend. Colorful depictions of the Night Horde MC put us right in the middle of their club. The Night Horde, while maintaining a stereotypical MC vibe, are interestingly different than any other MC I’ve read about. A fluid, moving, unique plot keeps up entranced as we enter this politically un-correct world of debauchery and mayhem. With a hero and heroine who enchant us with their character in a story that isn’t meant to enchant us, we see the world of Signal Bend in varying shades of grey rather than black and white. <br /><br />The character development in <i>Move the Sun</i> is the most intriguing element of the book. Lilli Accardo quite simply is a bad ass; smart, strong, sassy. She’s one of the most unique female leads I’ve had the pleasure of reading. Her courage, bravery, and sacrifice attribute to her overall beauty. This is a woman whom we should all respect. I adored her character and would stand in her corner any day. She’s one of my most favorite heroine’s I’ve ever read. The plot surrounding Lilli engrosses you fully with the nuances of mystery woven into her character development. The strength you come realize in this character based on the adversities she’s faced sets her apart from any other. The author takes into the past with interludes set inside the present story giving us further insight into Lilli. Isaac Lunden is amazing. I adored this character. He’s an older male lead with wisdom and a forthright sense of duty and establishment. While it is anti-establishment, Isaac rules with a humility and grace that personifies his entire being. Isaac respects the town he calls home and the residents of Signal Bend respect him dearly. He’s all the more attractive and alluring because of it. Lilli immediately sparks Isaac’s interest with her beauty and hot car. Isaac comes to understand Lilli as a partner he can not only respect but respects him with great admiration. She is taken almost immediately with Isaac as well. As we delve into the journey that is their relationship we find a perfect match made. The two of them together are refreshingly and brutally honest in with each other about everything they can share. The passion they share is explosive. Isaac and Lilli have found something in each other that they didn't even realize they were missing. <br /><br />All the elements worked brilliantly in <i>Move the Sun</i>; plot, conflict, characters. It’s a raw, gritty story. Descriptive prose about the town of Signal Bend, its people, and its business beautifully centered these two characters right to the epicenter of the story. Everything happening in the story is real; very telling of the kind of people Isaac and Lilli prove themselves to be. I'm excited to move on to the next book and see where their story goes from here as I’ve found a new series to add to the favorites list.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3758002299363059227" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('xpOtrdekac60Kp00kHauFsilsDxG7nlAdAjT60J51vjz4vKZ5cmiD5g8ABybbaTxJA5It8QFwE9kXBQwC9C60A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

She has skeletons too…\n\nEmmie Johansen has worked at the same horse farm all her life, and when the owner decides to sell, she’s crushed. Briar Hall is about to be sold to real estate developers, and she’s about to be out of a job, a home, and a purpose. \n\nEnter Walsh, and the Lean Dogs MC. Emmie thought losing the farm was the worst possible scenario. But when the club buys Briar Hall, and keeps her on as manager, she begins to unravel the farm’s dark secrets… and learns the true meaning of “outlaw.”\n\nThe Skeleton King is the third full-length installment of the Dartmoor Series, and is NOT a standalone novel.       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/7372898.Susan_Fanetti">About Susan Fanetti</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/7372898.Susan_Fanetti"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1452561234p3/7372898.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/7372898.Susan_Fanetti">Susan Fanetti
</a></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer16750642944625194486">I was born and raised in the Midwest, but I was transplanted into the dusty soil of Northern California and have apparently taken root there. An inveterate geek and gamer, I am a fan of many things considered pop culture and maybe even lowbrow.<br/><br/>As a reader, my favorite genres are science fiction and fantasy, but as a writer, I've found my home in romance--or perhaps it's better to say simply "love </span>
  <span id="freeText16750642944625194486" style="display:none">I was born and raised in the Midwest, but I was transplanted into the dusty soil of Northern California and have apparently taken root there. An inveterate geek and gamer, I am a fan of many things considered pop culture and maybe even lowbrow.<br /><br />As a reader, my favorite genres are science fiction and fantasy, but as a writer, I've found my home in romance--or perhaps it's better to say simply "love stories." I have a yen to try other genres, too, at some point, but for now my muse wants to tell stories about lovers and families.<br /><br />I write for the joy of it, and I write stories that I want to read. If others like them, too, that's just the cherry on top. I’m not interested in rules and formulae. I follow my muse and my characters and let them take me where they want to go, wherever that might be. I like big emotions, dark and light. <br /><br />I like complicated characters with flaws and weaknesses as well as strengths, and I like each character’s strengths and weaknesses to be different from those of other characters. I’m much more concerned that my characters be interesting and diverse than that they be widely considered to be likable. I try to create people, not types. <br /><br />Likewise, I want my stories each to be distinct from the others. Once I’ve told a story, I don’t want to tell it again. So even within a series, one of my books might be very different from the next. Some might be very dark, others equally mild.<br /><br />That isn’t to say there aren’t trends and recurrences in my work. I’m drawn to certain themes and settings, and my muse has her favorite toys and tools. But I guard against those tendencies becoming a formula.<br /><br />Find my blog at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.susanfanetti.com">www.susanfanetti.com</a><br /><br />Find my FB author page: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.facebook.com/authorsusanfanetti">https://www.facebook.com/authorsusanf...</a><br /><br />A note: I don't spend much time here on Goodreads. I try not to read any reviews of my own work. Besides, this is a site for readers, but since I write at a fairly manic pace, and read and edit for other writers, I don't have much time to read recreationally. Mainly, I log on to update my info. So if you message me here, it might be a while before I see it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16750642944625194486" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>

            if ($('bookCover_42479416').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_42479416').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>

</script>
